outputtype=string
default=Choose carefully!
val=0,Wasteland - a dead land filled with lava, dead trees and rocks.
val=1,Plateau - a platform of rock amidst a sea of lava with very few obstacles.
val=2,Sylvan Glade - an arena filled with trees that block line-of-sight.
val=3,Forsaken Quarry - an arena filled with small rocks that do not block line-of-sight.
val=4,Turrets - rangers and mages may like to ascend the many turrets in this arena to fire down at targets below.
val=5,Clan Cup Arena - adapted from the arena used in the 2013 Clan Cup.
val=6,Soggy Swamp - a waterlogged marshland filled with roots and rotten trees.
val=7,Ghastly Swamp - like the soggy swamp, but with aggressive ghasts to rot your food or steal your health.
val=8,Northleach Quell - a snowy area filled with sunken boats and broken bits of wood.
val=9,Gridlock - a huge 4-way multi-mountain map suited for KoTH modes with rangers and mages.
val=10,Ethereal - A strange realm in the clouds, with teleports to use and destroy.
val=11,Classic -  The original Clan Wars Classic.
val=12,Lumbridge Castle - the iconic castle and its courtyard.
val=13,Falador Park - the historic battleground.
